Many different business conceptualizations exist; Osterwalder's work and thesis propose a single reference model based on the similarities of a wide range of business model conceptualizations. With his business model design template, an enterprise can easily describe their business model.\r\nPartner Network: The business alliances which complement other aspects of the business model.\r\nKey Activities: The activities necessary to execute a company's business model.\r\nKey Resources: The resources that are necessary to create value for the customer.\r\nValue Proposition:The products and services a business offers.
